        var TL = {};
        var TL_NAMESPACE = function(){
            var props = {};
            var pub = {};

            function get(name){
                return props[name];
            } 
            function set(name,val){
                props[name] = val;
                return;
            }

            pub.get = get;
            pub.set = set;
            pub.init = function(init_fn){
                var new_public_accessors = init_fn(get,set);
                for(var i in new_public_accessors){
                    if(new_public_accessors.hasOwnProperty(i)){
                        pub[i] = new_public_accessors[i];
                    }
                }
            };     
            return pub;
        };

;(function($) {

$.fn._fadeIn = $.fn.fadeIn;

var noOp = function() {};

// this bit is to ensure we don't call setExpression when we shouldn't (with extra muscle to handle
// retarded userAgent strings on Vista)
var mode = document.documentMode || 0;
var setExpr = $.browser.msie &amp;&amp; (($.browser.version &lt; 8 &amp;&amp; !mode) || mode &lt; 8);
var ie6 = $.browser.msie &amp;&amp; /MSIE 6.0/.test(navigator.userAgent) &amp;&amp; !mode;

// global $ methods for blocking/unblocking the entire page
$.blockUI   = function(opts) { install(window, opts); };
$.unblockUI = function(opts) { remove(window, opts); };

// convenience method for quick growl-like notifications  (http://www.google.com/search?q=growl)
$.growlUI = function(title, message, timeout, onClose) {
	var $m = $('&lt;div class="growlUI"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
	if (title) $m.append('&lt;h1&gt;'+title+'&lt;/h1&gt;');
	if (message) $m.append('&lt;h2&gt;'+message+'&lt;/h2&gt;');
	if (timeout == undefined) timeout = 3000;
	$.blockUI({
		message: $m, fadeIn: 700, fadeOut: 1000, centerY: false,
		timeout: timeout, showOverlay: false,
		onUnblock: onClose, 
		css: $.blockUI.defaults.growlCSS
	});
};

// plugin method for blocking element content
$.fn.block = function(opts) {
	return this.unblock({ fadeOut: 0 }).each(function() {
		if ($.css(this,'position') == 'static')
			this.style.position = 'relative';
		if ($.browser.msie)
			this.style.zoom = 1; // force 'hasLayout'
		install(this, opts);
	});
};

// plugin method for unblocking element content
$.fn.unblock = function(opts) {
	return this.each(function() {
		remove(this, opts);
	});
};

$.blockUI.version = 2.35; // 2nd generation blocking at no extra cost!

// override these in your code to change the default behavior and style
$.blockUI.defaults = {
	// message displayed when blocking (use null for no message)
	message:  '&lt;h1&gt;Please wait...&lt;/h1&gt;',

	title: null,	  // title string; only used when theme == true
	draggable: true,  // only used when theme == true (requires jquery-ui.js to be loaded)
	
	theme: false, // set to true to use with jQuery UI themes
	
	// styles for the message when blocking; if you wish to disable
	// these and use an external stylesheet then do this in your code:
	// $.blockUI.defaults.css = {};
	css: {
		padding:	0,
		margin:		0,
		width:		'30%',
		top:		'40%',
		left:		'35%',
		textAlign:	'center',
		color:		'#000',
		border:		'3px solid #aaa',
		backgroundColor:'#fff',
		cursor:		'wait'
	},
	
	// minimal style set used when themes are used
	themedCSS: {
		width:	'30%',
		top:	'40%',
		left:	'35%'
	},

	// styles for the overlay
	overlayCSS:  {
		backgroundColor: '#000',
		opacity:	  	 0.6,
		cursor:		  	 'wait'
	},

	// styles applied when using $.growlUI
	growlCSS: {
		width:  	'350px',
		top:		'10px',
		left:   	'',
		right:  	'10px',
		border: 	'none',
		padding:	'5px',
		opacity:	0.6,
		cursor: 	'default',
		color:		'#fff',
		backgroundColor: '#000',
		'-webkit-border-radius': '10px',
		'-moz-border-radius':	 '10px',
		'border-radius': 		 '10px'
	},
	
	// IE issues: 'about:blank' fails on HTTPS and javascript:false is s-l-o-w
	// (hat tip to Jorge H. N. de Vasconcelos)
	iframeSrc: /^https/i.test(window.location.href || '') ? 'javascript:false' : 'about:blank',

	// force usage of iframe in non-IE browsers (handy for blocking applets)
	forceIframe: false,

	// z-index for the blocking overlay
	baseZ: 1000,

	// set these to true to have the message automatically centered
	centerX: true, // &lt;-- only effects element blocking (page block controlled via css above)
	centerY: true,

	// allow body element to be stetched in ie6; this makes blocking look better
	// on "short" pages.  disable if you wish to prevent changes to the body height
	allowBodyStretch: true,

	// enable if you want key and mouse events to be disabled for content that is blocked
	bindEvents: true,

	// be default blockUI will supress tab navigation from leaving blocking content
	// (if bindEvents is true)
	constrainTabKey: true,

	// fadeIn time in millis; set to 0 to disable fadeIn on block
	fadeIn:  200,

	// fadeOut time in millis; set to 0 to disable fadeOut on unblock
	fadeOut:  400,

	// time in millis to wait before auto-unblocking; set to 0 to disable auto-unblock
	timeout: 0,

	// disable if you don't want to show the overlay
	showOverlay: true,

	// if true, focus will be placed in the first available input field when
	// page blocking
	focusInput: true,

	// if true, focus will be placed in the first available blank input field when page blocking
	focusBlankInput: false,

	// suppresses the use of overlay styles on FF/Linux (due to performance issues with opacity)
	applyPlatformOpacityRules: true,
	
	// callback method invoked when fadeIn has completed and blocking message is visible
	onBlock: null,

	// callback method invoked when unblocking has completed; the callback is
	// passed the element that has been unblocked (which is the window object for page
	// blocks) and the options that were passed to the unblock call:
	//	 onUnblock(element, options)
	onUnblock: null,

	// don't ask; if you really must know: http://groups.google.com/group/jquery-en/browse_thread/thread/36640a8730503595/2f6a79a77a78e493#2f6a79a77a78e493
	quirksmodeOffsetHack: 4,

	// class name of the message block
	blockMsgClass: 'blockMsg'
};

// private data and functions follow...

var pageBlock = null;
var pageBlockEls = [];

function install(el, opts) {
	var full = (el == window);
	var msg = opts &amp;&amp; opts.message !== undefined ? opts.message : undefined;
	opts = $.extend({}, $.blockUI.defaults, opts || {});
	opts.overlayCSS = $.extend({}, $.blockUI.defaults.overlayCSS, opts.overlayCSS || {});
	var css = $.extend({}, $.blockUI.defaults.css, opts.css || {});
	var themedCSS = $.extend({}, $.blockUI.defaults.themedCSS, opts.themedCSS || {});
	msg = msg === undefined ? opts.message : msg;

	// remove the current block (if there is one)
	if (full &amp;&amp; pageBlock)
		remove(window, {fadeOut:0});

	// if an existing element is being used as the blocking content then we capture
	// its current place in the DOM (and current display style) so we can restore
	// it when we unblock
	if (msg &amp;&amp; typeof msg != 'string' &amp;&amp; (msg.parentNode || msg.jquery)) {
		var node = msg.jquery ? msg[0] : msg;
        if (node) {
            var data = {};
            $(el).data('blockUI.history', data);
            data.el = node;
            data.parent = node.parentNode;
            data.display = node.style.display;
            data.position = node.style.position;
            if (data.parent)
                data.parent.removeChild(node);
        }
    }
	var z = opts.baseZ;

	// blockUI uses 3 layers for blocking, for simplicity they are all used on every platform;
	// layer1 is the iframe layer which is used to supress bleed through of underlying content
	// layer2 is the overlay layer which has opacity and a wait cursor (by default)
	// layer3 is the message content that is displayed while blocking

	var lyr1 = ($.browser.msie || opts.forceIframe) 
		? $('&lt;iframe class="blockUI" style="z-index:'+ (z++) +';display:none;border:none;margin:0;padding:0;position:absolute;width:100%;height:100%;top:0;left:0" src="'+opts.iframeSrc+'"&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;')
		: $('&lt;div class="blockUI" style="display:none"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
	var lyr2 = $('&lt;div class="blockUI blockOverlay" style="z-index:'+ (z++) +';display:none;border:none;margin:0;padding:0;width:100%;height:100%;top:0;left:0"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
	
	var lyr3, s;
	if (opts.theme &amp;&amp; full) {
		s = '&lt;div class="blockUI ' + opts.blockMsgClass + ' blockPage ui-dialog ui-widget ui-corner-all" style="z-index:'+z+';display:none;position:fixed"&gt;' +
				'&lt;div class="ui-widget-header ui-dialog-titlebar ui-corner-all blockTitle"&gt;'+(opts.title || '&nbsp;')+'&lt;/div&gt;' +
				'&lt;div class="ui-widget-content ui-dialog-content"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
			'&lt;/div&gt;';
	}
	else if (opts.theme) {
		s = '&lt;div class="blockUI ' + opts.blockMsgClass + ' blockElement ui-dialog ui-widget ui-corner-all" style="z-index:'+z+';display:none;position:absolute"&gt;' +
				'&lt;div class="ui-widget-header ui-dialog-titlebar ui-corner-all blockTitle"&gt;'+(opts.title || '&nbsp;')+'&lt;/div&gt;' +
				'&lt;div class="ui-widget-content ui-dialog-content"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;' +
			'&lt;/div&gt;';
	}
	else if (full) {
		s = '&lt;div class="blockUI ' + opts.blockMsgClass + ' blockPage" style="z-index:'+z+';display:none;position:fixed"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
	}			
	else {
		s = '&lt;div class="blockUI ' + opts.blockMsgClass + ' blockElement" style="z-index:'+z+';display:none;position:absolute"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
	}
	lyr3 = $(s);

	// if we have a message, style it
	if (msg) {
		if (opts.theme) {
			lyr3.css(themedCSS);
			lyr3.addClass('ui-widget-content');
		}
		else 
			lyr3.css(css);
	}

	// style the overlay
	if (!opts.applyPlatformOpacityRules || !($.browser.mozilla &amp;&amp; /Linux/.test(navigator.platform)))
		lyr2.css(opts.overlayCSS);
	lyr2.css('position', full ? 'fixed' : 'absolute');

	// make iframe layer transparent in IE
	if ($.browser.msie || opts.forceIframe)
		lyr1.css('opacity',0.0);

	//$([lyr1[0],lyr2[0],lyr3[0]]).appendTo(full ? 'body' : el);
	var layers = [lyr1,lyr2,lyr3], $par = full ? $('body') : $(el);
	$.each(layers, function() {
		this.appendTo($par);
	});
	
	if (opts.theme &amp;&amp; opts.draggable &amp;&amp; $.fn.draggable) {
		lyr3.draggable({
			handle: '.ui-dialog-titlebar',
			cancel: 'li'
		});
	}

	// ie7 must use absolute positioning in quirks mode and to account for activex issues (when scrolling)
	var expr = setExpr &amp;&amp; (!$.boxModel || $('object,embed', full ? null : el).length &gt; 0);
	if (ie6 || expr) {
		// give body 100% height
		if (full &amp;&amp; opts.allowBodyStretch &amp;&amp; $.boxModel)
			$('html,body').css('height','100%');

		// fix ie6 issue when blocked element has a border width
		if ((ie6 || !$.boxModel) &amp;&amp; !full) {
			var t = sz(el,'borderTopWidth'), l = sz(el,'borderLeftWidth');
			var fixT = t ? '(0 - '+t+')' : 0;
			var fixL = l ? '(0 - '+l+')' : 0;
		}

		// simulate fixed position
		$.each([lyr1,lyr2,lyr3], function(i,o) {
			var s = o[0].style;
			s.position = 'absolute';
			if (i &lt; 2) {
				full ? s.setExpression('height','Math.max(document.body.scrollHeight, document.body.offsetHeight) - (jQuery.boxModel?0:'+opts.quirksmodeOffsetHack+') + "px"')
					 : s.setExpression('height','this.parentNode.offsetHeight + "px"');
				full ? s.setExpression('width','jQuery.boxModel &amp;&amp; document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth + "px"')
					 : s.setExpression('width','this.parentNode.offsetWidth + "px"');
				if (fixL) s.setExpression('left', fixL);
				if (fixT) s.setExpression('top', fixT);
			}
			else if (opts.centerY) {
				if (full) s.setExpression('top','(document.documentElement.clientHeight || document.body.clientHeight) / 2 - (this.offsetHeight / 2) + (blah = document.documentElement.scrollTop ? document.documentElement.scrollTop : document.body.scrollTop) + "px"');
				s.marginTop = 0;
			}
			else if (!opts.centerY &amp;&amp; full) {
				var top = (opts.css &amp;&amp; opts.css.top) ? parseInt(opts.css.top) : 0;
				var expression = '((document.documentElement.scrollTop ? document.documentElement.scrollTop : document.body.scrollTop) + '+top+') + "px"';
				s.setExpression('top',expression);
			}
		});
	}

	// show the message
	if (msg) {
		if (opts.theme)
			lyr3.find('.ui-widget-content').append(msg);
		else
			lyr3.append(msg);
		if (msg.jquery || msg.nodeType)
			$(msg).show();
	}

	if (($.browser.msie || opts.forceIframe) &amp;&amp; opts.showOverlay)
		lyr1.show(); // opacity is zero
	if (opts.fadeIn) {
		var cb = opts.onBlock ? opts.onBlock : noOp;
		var cb1 = (opts.showOverlay &amp;&amp; !msg) ? cb : noOp;
		var cb2 = msg ? cb : noOp;
		if (opts.showOverlay)
			lyr2._fadeIn(opts.fadeIn, cb1);
		if (msg)
			lyr3._fadeIn(opts.fadeIn, cb2);
	}
	else {
		if (opts.showOverlay)
			lyr2.show();
		if (msg)
			lyr3.show();
		if (opts.onBlock)
			opts.onBlock();
	}

	// bind key and mouse events
	bind(1, el, opts);

	if (full) {
		pageBlock = lyr3[0];
		pageBlockEls = $(':input:enabled:visible',pageBlock);
		if (opts.focusBlankInput) {
            var focused = false;
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; pageBlockEls.length; i++) {
                if ($(pageBlockEls[i]).attr('id') != '' &amp;&amp; $(pageBlockEls[i]).val() == '') {
                    $(pageBlockEls[i]).focus();
                    focused = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!focused) {
    			setTimeout(focus, 20);
            }
        } else if (opts.focusInput) {
			setTimeout(focus, 20);
        }
	}
	else
		center(lyr3[0], opts.centerX, opts.centerY);

	if (opts.timeout) {
		// auto-unblock
		var to = setTimeout(function() {
			full ? $.unblockUI(opts) : $(el).unblock(opts);
		}, opts.timeout);
		$(el).data('blockUI.timeout', to);
	}
};

// remove the block
function remove(el, opts) {
	var full = (el == window);
	var $el = $(el);
	var data = $el.data('blockUI.history');
	var to = $el.data('blockUI.timeout');
	if (to) {
		clearTimeout(to);
		$el.removeData('blockUI.timeout');
	}
	opts = $.extend({}, $.blockUI.defaults, opts || {});
	bind(0, el, opts); // unbind events
	
	var els;
	if (full) // crazy selector to handle odd field errors in ie6/7
		els = $('body').children().filter('.blockUI').add('body &gt; .blockUI');
	else
		els = $('.blockUI', el);

	if (full)
		pageBlock = pageBlockEls = null;

	if (opts.fadeOut) {
		els.fadeOut(opts.fadeOut);
		setTimeout(function() { reset(els,data,opts,el); }, opts.fadeOut);
	}
	else
		reset(els, data, opts, el);
};

// move blocking element back into the DOM where it started
function reset(els,data,opts,el) {
	els.each(function(i,o) {
		// remove via DOM calls so we don't lose event handlers
		if (this.parentNode)
			this.parentNode.removeChild(this);
	});

	if (data &amp;&amp; data.el) {
		data.el.style.display = data.display;
		data.el.style.position = data.position;
		if (data.parent)
			data.parent.appendChild(data.el);
		$(el).removeData('blockUI.history');
	}

	if (typeof opts.onUnblock == 'function')
		opts.onUnblock(el,opts);
};

// bind/unbind the handler
function bind(b, el, opts) {
	var full = el == window, $el = $(el);

	// don't bother unbinding if there is nothing to unbind
	if (!b &amp;&amp; (full &amp;&amp; !pageBlock || !full &amp;&amp; !$el.data('blockUI.isBlocked')))
		return;
	if (!full)
		$el.data('blockUI.isBlocked', b);

	// don't bind events when overlay is not in use or if bindEvents is false
	if (!opts.bindEvents || (b &amp;&amp; !opts.showOverlay)) 
		return;

	// bind anchors and inputs for mouse and key events
	var events = 'mousedown mouseup keydown keypress';
	b ? $(document).bind(events, opts, handler) : $(document).unbind(events, handler);

// former impl...
//	   var $e = $('a,:input');
//	   b ? $e.bind(events, opts, handler) : $e.unbind(events, handler);
};

// event handler to suppress keyboard/mouse events when blocking
function handler(e) {
	// allow tab navigation (conditionally)
	if (e.keyCode &amp;&amp; e.keyCode == 9) {
		if (pageBlock &amp;&amp; e.data.constrainTabKey) {
			var els = pageBlockEls;
			var fwd = !e.shiftKey &amp;&amp; e.target === els[els.length-1];
			var back = e.shiftKey &amp;&amp; e.target === els[0];
			if (fwd || back) {
				setTimeout(function(){focus(back)},10);
				return false;
			}
		}
	}
	var opts = e.data;
	// allow events within the message content
	if ($(e.target).parents('div.' + opts.blockMsgClass).length &gt; 0)
		return true;

	// allow events for content that is not being blocked
	return $(e.target).parents().children().filter('div.blockUI').length == 0;
};

function focus(back) {
	if (!pageBlockEls)
		return;
	var e = pageBlockEls[back===true ? pageBlockEls.length-1 : 0];
	if (e)
		e.focus();
};

function center(el, x, y) {
	var p = el.parentNode, s = el.style;
	var l = ((p.offsetWidth - el.offsetWidth)/2) - sz(p,'borderLeftWidth');
	var t = ((p.offsetHeight - el.offsetHeight)/2) - sz(p,'borderTopWidth');
    // Should never be negative; if it is, the parent hasn't loaded yet -- hardcode default for listing centering
	if (x) s.left = l &lt; 0 ? '95.5px' : (l+'px');
	if (y) s.top  = t &gt; 0 ? (t+'px') : '0';
};

function sz(el, p) {
	return parseInt($.css(el,p))||0;
};

})(jQuery);

.insertAfter(el),buttonlabel=(this.buttonlabel=$('&lt;span /&gt;'))
.html(o.noneSelectedText)
.appendTo(button),menu=(this.menu=$('&lt;div /&gt;'))
.addClass('ui-multiselect-menu ui-widget ui-widget-content ui-corner-all')
.addClass(o.classes)
.insertAfter(button),header=(this.header=$('&lt;div /&gt;'))

.html(function(){if(o.header===true){return'';}else if(typeof o.header==="string"){return'&lt;li class="ui-helper-reset-element"&gt;'+o.header+'&lt;/li&gt;';}else{return'';}})
.append('&lt;li class="ui-multiselect-close"&gt;&lt;a href="#" class="ui-multiselect-close"&gt;&lt;span class="ui-icon ui-icon-circle-close"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;')
.appendTo(header),checkboxContainer=(this.checkboxContainer=$('&lt;ul /&gt;'))

if(isSelected&amp;&amp;!o.multiple){labelClasses.push('ui-state-active');}

this.buttonlabel.html(value);return value;},_bindEvents:function(){var self=this,button=this.button;function clickHandler(){self[self._isOpen?'close':'open']();$('#largeSetInput').focus();return false;}
button

function calcMP(){if(!($('#calc_mp'))){return;}
var Vprice=$('#calc_pp').val().replace(/[^\d\.]/g,"");if(Vprice!=''&amp;&amp;Vprice.split(".").length&lt;=2){var Vdown=Vprice*$('#calc_dp').val();var Vrate=$('#calc_apr').val();var Vyears=30;var Vprincipal=eval(Vprice)-eval(Vdown);var Vpmts=Vyears*12;var Vpayment=computeMonthlyPayment(Vprincipal,Vpmts,Vrate);$('#calc_mp').html("$"+formatNumberDec(Vpayment,2,1));if($('#listing-estimated-payment'))$('#listing-estimated-payment').html("$"+formatNumberDec(Vpayment,2,1));}else{$('#calc_mp').html('');if($('#listing-estimated-payment'))$('#listing-estimated-payment').html('');}}
function computeMonthlyPayment(prin,numPmts,intRate){var pmtAmt=0;if(intRate==0){pmtAmt=prin/numPmts;}else{if(intRate&gt;=1.0){intRate=intRate/100.0;}
intRate/=12;var pow=1;for(var j=0;j&lt;numPmts;j++){pow=pow*(1+intRate);}
pmtAmt=(prin*pow*intRate)/(pow-1);}
return pmtAmt;}
function computeMonthlyPaymentSA(prin,years,intRate){var compInt=Math.pow(1+intRate/2,1/6)-1;return(Math.round(100*prin*compInt*Math.pow(1+compInt,12*years)/(Math.pow(1+compInt,12*years)-1))/100).toFixed(2);}
function formatNumberDec(num,places,comma){var isNeg=0;if(num&lt;0){num=num*-1;isNeg=1;}
var myDecFact=1;var myPlaces=0;var myZeros="";while(myPlaces&lt;places){myDecFact=myDecFact*10;myPlaces=eval(myPlaces)+eval(1);myZeros=myZeros+"0";}
onum=Math.round(num*myDecFact)/myDecFact;integer=Math.floor(onum);if(Math.ceil(onum)==integer){decimal=myZeros;}else{decimal=Math.round((onum-integer)*myDecFact);}
decimal=decimal.toString();if(decimal.length&lt;places){fillZeroes=places-decimal.length;for(z=0;z&lt;fillZeroes;z++){decimal="0"+decimal;}}
if(places&gt;0){decimal="."+decimal;}
if(comma==1){integer=integer.toString();var tmpnum="";var tmpinteger="";var y=0;for(x=integer.length;x&gt;0;x--){tmpnum=tmpnum+integer.charAt(x-1);y=y+1;if(y==3&amp;x&gt;1){tmpnum=tmpnum+",";y=0;}}
for(x=tmpnum.length;x&gt;0;x--){tmpinteger=tmpinteger+tmpnum.charAt(x-1);}
finNum=tmpinteger+""+decimal;}else{finNum=integer+""+decimal;}
if(isNeg==1){finNum="-"+finNum;}
return finNum;}

else{$("#add_to_favorites").show();$("#remove_from_favorites").hide();}}}

function reset_controls(mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft){if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){mapWidth=typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:656;mapHeight=typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:382;mapMarginTop=typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:-392;mapMarginLeft=typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0;$('#map_canvas').width(mapWidth);$('#map_canvas').height(mapHeight);$('#map_canvas').css("marginTop",mapMarginTop+"px");$('#map_canvas').css("marginLeft",mapMarginLeft+"px");var myOptions={showMapTypeSelector:true,mapTypeId:Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road}
if(get('latlngbounds')!==undefined){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))});setTimeout(function(){if(TL.maps.get('map').getZoom()&lt;=3){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))})}},1000);setTimeout(function(){if(TL.maps.get('map').getZoom()&lt;=3){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))})}},4000);}else{get('map').setView({center:get('map').getCenter(),animate:false});}}else{mapWidth=typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:652;mapHeight=typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:190;mapMarginTop=typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:0;mapMarginLeft=typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0;$('#map_canvas').width(mapWidth);$('#map_canvas').height(mapHeight);$('#map_canvas').css("marginTop",mapMarginTop+"px");$('#map_canvas').css("marginLeft",mapMarginLeft+"px");var myOptions={showMapTypeSelector:false,mapTypeId:Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road}
get('map').setView({center:get('map').getCenter(),animate:false});}
get('map').setOptions(myOptions);}
function reset_markers(){var markers=get('markers');var infowindows=get('infowindows');close_all_infowindows();if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){for(i=0;i&lt;markers.length;i++){if(markers[i]){markers[i].setOptions({visible:true});}}
get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(get('latlngbounds'))});}else{var listing_counter=get('map_selector').replace(/([^\d]*)/,"");for(i=0;i&lt;markers.length;i++){if(markers[i]){if(i==listing_counter-1){markers[i].setOptions({visible:true});var latLng=markers[i].getLocation();get('map').setView({zoom:14,center:latLng});}else{markers[i].setOptions({visible:false});}}}}}
function loadmap(selector,mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft){set('map_selector',selector);var infowindows=get('infowindows');if(selector=='map_container'){$('#gmap-hidden').hide();$('#gmap-shown').show();for(i=1;i&lt;=10;i++){TL.maps.hidemap('listing_map_container_'+i);}}else{var listing_counter=selector.replace(/([^\d]*)/,"");for(i=1;i&lt;=10;i++){if(i!=listing_counter){TL.maps.hidemap('listing_map_container_'+i);}}
TL.maps.hidemap('map_container');$('#view-map-text-'+listing_counter).hide();$('#view-map-icon-'+listing_counter).hide();$('#search-listing-map-'+listing_counter).show();}
$('#'+selector).show();$('#map_canvas').appendTo('#'+selector);$('#map_on').val(1);if(get('maploaded')){TL.maps.reset_controls(mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft);TL.maps.reset_markers();}else{if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){set('map_width',typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:656);set('map_height',typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:382);set('map_margin_top',typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:-392);set('map_margin_left',typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0);}else{set('map_width',typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:652);set('map_height',typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:190);set('map_margin_top',typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:0);set('map_margin_left',typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0);}

function close_all_infowindows(){var infowindows=get('infowindows');for(i=0;i&lt;=infowindows.length-1;i++){if(infowindows[i]){infowindows[i].setOptions({visible:false});}}}

function InfoWindowHtml(id,counter,price,addr1,addr2,img_uri,base_virtual_uri,address_displayable,geo_p,display_address,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,search_map,extra_info,agent_office){var content;var message='';if(address_displayable){if(geo_p!='address'){message='Unable to map this location. Here is the closest '+geo_p+'.';}}else{addr1='';addr2='';message="The local MLS board does not permit the display of this address.  Here is the closest address we are allowed to display: ";}
content=info_window_content(id,counter,price,addr1,addr2,img_uri,message,base_virtual_uri,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,search_map,extra_info,agent_office);return content;}
function loadDetailMap(){if(get('maploaded')){initDetailMap();return;}

function targetMap(map,lat,lon,info_html){var latlon=new Microsoft.Maps.Location(lat,lon);set('point',latlon);map.setView({centerOffset:new Microsoft.Maps.Point(-15,20),center:latlon})
var pushpinOptions={icon:'/static/images/maps/regular.png',width:22,height:25,typeName:'pushpin'};var pushpin=new Microsoft.Maps.Pushpin(get('point'),pushpinOptions);var infoboxOptions={width:350,height:103,description:info_html,showCloseButton:true,showPointer:true,offset:new Microsoft.Maps.Point(0,18)};var infobox=new Microsoft.Maps.Infobox(latlon,infoboxOptions);Microsoft.Maps.Events.addHandler(pushpin,'click',function(){infobox.setOptions({visible:true});});map.entities.push(pushpin);map.entities.push(infobox);}

$.getJSON("http://dev.virtualearth.net/REST/v1/Locations/"+encodeURIComponent(geo_address)+'?jsonp=?&amp;key='+get('bing_key'),function(data){if(data&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].matchCodes[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].matchCodes[0]=='Good'){var message=InfoWindowHtml(listing_id,-1,display_price,addr_line1,addr_line2,map_image,'/listing/from_listing_map',address_displayable,geo_precision,display_address,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,0,ga_extra_info,'');targetMap(map_detail,parseFloat(data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].point.coordinates[0]),parseFloat(data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].point.coordinates[1]),message);return;}else{$.getJSON("http://dev.virtualearth.net/REST/v1/Locations/"+encodeURIComponent(geo_zip)+'?jsonp=?&amp;key='+get('bing_key'),function(data){if(data&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].matchCodes[0]&amp;&amp;data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].matchCodes[0]=='Good'){var message="&lt;div style=\'width:200px; text-align:left; font-size:.9em;\'&gt;Address not found...mapping zip: "+geo_zip+"&lt;/div&gt;";targetMap(map_detail,parseFloat(data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].point.coordinates[0]),parseFloat(data.resourceSets[0].resources[0].point.coordinates[1]),message);return;}});}});}}

function reset_controls(mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft){if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){mapWidth=typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:656;mapHeight=typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:382;mapMarginTop=typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:-392;mapMarginLeft=typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0;$('#map_canvas').width(mapWidth);$('#map_canvas').height(mapHeight);$('#map_canvas').css("marginTop",mapMarginTop+"px");$('#map_canvas').css("marginLeft",mapMarginLeft+"px");var myOptions={showMapTypeSelector:true,mapTypeId:Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road}
if(get('latlngbounds')!==undefined){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))});setTimeout(function(){if(TL.maps.get('map').getZoom()&lt;=3){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))})}},1000);setTimeout(function(){if(TL.maps.get('map').getZoom()&lt;=3){TL.maps.get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(TL.maps.get('latlngbounds'))})}},4000);}else{get('map').setView({center:get('map').getCenter(),animate:false});}}else{mapWidth=typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:652;mapHeight=typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:190;mapMarginTop=typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:0;mapMarginLeft=typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0;$('#map_canvas').width(mapWidth);$('#map_canvas').height(mapHeight);$('#map_canvas').css("marginTop",mapMarginTop+"px");$('#map_canvas').css("marginLeft",mapMarginLeft+"px");var myOptions={showMapTypeSelector:false,mapTypeId:Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road}
get('map').setView({center:get('map').getCenter(),animate:false});}
get('map').setOptions(myOptions);}
function reset_markers(){var markers=get('markers');var infowindows=get('infowindows');close_all_infowindows();if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){for(i=0;i&lt;markers.length;i++){if(markers[i]){markers[i].setOptions({visible:true});}}
get('map').setView({bounds:Microsoft.Maps.LocationRect.fromLocations(get('latlngbounds'))});}else{var listing_counter=get('map_selector').replace(/([^\d]*)/,"");for(i=0;i&lt;markers.length;i++){if(markers[i]){if(i==listing_counter-1){markers[i].setOptions({visible:true});var latLng=markers[i].getLocation();get('map').setView({zoom:14,center:latLng});}else{markers[i].setOptions({visible:false});}}}}}
function loadmap(selector,mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft){set('map_selector',selector);var infowindows=get('infowindows');if(selector=='map_container'){$('#gmap-hidden').hide();$('#gmap-shown').show();for(i=1;i&lt;=10;i++){TL.maps.hidemap('listing_map_container_'+i);}}else{var listing_counter=selector.replace(/([^\d]*)/,"");for(i=1;i&lt;=10;i++){if(i!=listing_counter){TL.maps.hidemap('listing_map_container_'+i);}}
TL.maps.hidemap('map_container');$('#view-map-text-'+listing_counter).hide();$('#view-map-icon-'+listing_counter).hide();$('#search-listing-map-'+listing_counter).show();}
$('#'+selector).show();$('#map_canvas').appendTo('#'+selector);$('#map_on').val(1);if(get('maploaded')){TL.maps.reset_controls(mapWidth,mapHeight,mapMarginTop,mapMarginLeft);TL.maps.reset_markers();}else{if(get('map_selector')=='map_container'){set('map_width',typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:656);set('map_height',typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:382);set('map_margin_top',typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:-392);set('map_margin_left',typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0);}else{set('map_width',typeof(mapWidth)!='undefined'?mapWidth:652);set('map_height',typeof(mapHeight)!='undefined'?mapHeight:190);set('map_margin_top',typeof(mapMarginTop)!='undefined'?mapMarginTop:0);set('map_margin_left',typeof(mapMarginLeft)!='undefined'?mapMarginLeft:0);}
var script=document.createElement("script");script.type="text/javascript";script.src="http://ecn.dev.virtualearth.net/mapcontrol/mapcontrol.ashx?v=7.0&amp;onScriptLoad=mapInitCallback";document.body.appendChild(script);}
set('maploaded',true);}
function close_all_infowindows(){var infowindows=get('infowindows');for(i=0;i&lt;=infowindows.length-1;i++){if(infowindows[i]){infowindows[i].setOptions({visible:false});}}}
function hidemap(selector){if(selector=='map_container'){$('#gmap-hidden').show();$('#gmap-shown').hide();}else{var listing_counter=selector.replace(/([^\d]*)/,"");$('#view-map-text-'+listing_counter).show();$('#view-map-icon-'+listing_counter).show();$('#search-listing-map-'+listing_counter).hide();}
$('#'+selector).hide();$('#map_on').val('');}
function info_window_content(id,counter,price,addr1,addr2,img_uri,message,base_virtual_uri,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,search_map,extra_info,agent_office){var content='&lt;div style="height:'+(search_map==1?'132':'105')+'px;overflow:hidden;"&gt;'+

content+="&lt;div class='idxlogo'&gt;"+idx_logo+"&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style='clear:both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;";if(addr1!=''){content+='&lt;div style="float:left;margin-left:6px;"&gt;&lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="'+"TL.main.detail_click("+id+", "+JSON.stringify(search_data).replace(/"/g,"'")+"); return false;"+'" class="listing-detail-link" style="text-decoration:none;color:#555555;"&gt;&lt;font style="text-decoration:none;color:#555555;font-size:11px;"&gt;&lt;nobr&gt;'+addr1+'&lt;/nobr&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="clear:both;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';}
if(addr2!=''){content+='&lt;div style="float:left;margin-left:6px;"&gt;&lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="'+"TL.main.detail_click("+id+", "+JSON.stringify(search_data).replace(/"/g,"'")+"); return false;"+'" class="listing-detail-link" style="text-decoration:none;color:#555555;"&gt;&lt;font style="text-decoration:none;color:#555555;font-size:11px;"&gt;&lt;nobr&gt;'+addr2+'&lt;/nobr&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="clear:both;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';}
content+="&lt;div style='margin-left:6px;'&gt;&lt;font style='font-weight:bold'&gt;"+bedrooms+"&lt;/font&gt; Bedrooms / &lt;font style='font-weight:bold'&gt;"+bathrooms+"&lt;/font&gt; Baths&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style='clear:both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;";content+="&lt;div style='margin-left:6px;'&gt;&lt;font style='font-weight:bold'&gt;"+square_feet+"&lt;/font&gt; Sq. Ft. / ";content+="MLS #"+mls_number+"&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style='clear:both;'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;";if(search_map){content+='&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td colspan=2 align=center&gt;&lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" onClick="'+"TL.main.detail_click("+id+", "+JSON.stringify(search_data).replace(/"/g,"'")+"); return false;"+'" class="listing-detail-link" style="display:block; border:1px solid #eaeaea; background-color:#D4F0FF; line-height:150%; font-weight:bold; padding:3px;"&gt;View Full Details &amp; '+images_count+' Full Size Photos&lt;/a&gt;';}

function InfoWindowHtml(id,counter,price,addr1,addr2,img_uri,base_virtual_uri,address_displayable,geo_p,display_address,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,search_map,extra_info,agent_office){var content;var message='';if(address_displayable){if(geo_p!='address'){message='Unable to map this location. Here is the closest '+geo_p+'.';}}else{addr1='';addr2='';message="The local MLS board does not permit the display of this address.  Here is the closest address we are allowed to display: ";}
content=info_window_content(id,counter,price,addr1,addr2,img_uri,message,base_virtual_uri,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,search_map,extra_info,agent_office);return content;}
function loadDetailMap(){if(get('maploaded')){initDetailMap();return;}
var script=document.createElement("script");script.type="text/javascript";script.src="http://ecn.dev.virtualearth.net/mapcontrol/mapcontrol.ashx?v=7.0&amp;onScriptLoad=mapInitDetailCallback";document.body.appendChild(script);setTimeout(function(){if(TL.maps.get('map_detail')===undefined){TL.maps.initDetailMap()}},3000);function mapInitDetailCallback(){TL.maps.initDetailMap();}}
function targetMap(map,lat,lon,info_html){var latlon=new Microsoft.Maps.Location(lat,lon);set('point',latlon);map.setView({centerOffset:new Microsoft.Maps.Point(-15,20),center:latlon})

function initDetailMap(){var map_detail;if(document.getElementById("map_detail")){set('map_detail',new Microsoft.Maps.Map(document.getElementById("map_detail"),{credentials:get('bing_key'),zoom:13,mapTypeId:Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road,showMapTypeSelector:false}));map_detail=get('map_detail');Microsoft.Maps.Events.addHandler(get('map'),'mousewheel',function(e){e.handled=true;return true;});if(get_query_string('favs')=='1'){$('#map_detail').width(912);$('#map_detail').height(412);map_detail.setView({center:map_detail.getCenter(),animate:false});}

function setBirdsEyeView(set_value){if(set_value){$('#map_bird').show();}else{$('#map_bird').hide();}}
function setMapTypeView(map_type){var map_detail=get('map_detail');if(map_detail){$('#map_tabs li a').removeClass("here");current_map_type=map_type;if(map_type=='road'){$('#map_detail').show();$('#bmap').hide();map_detail.setMapType(Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.road);}else if(map_type=='aerial'){$('#map_detail').show();$('#bmap').hide();map_detail.setMapType(Microsoft.Maps.MapTypeId.aerial);}else if(map_type=='bird'){if(get('birds_eye_setup')===false){set('birds_eye_setup',true);loadBMap();}
$('#bmap').show();$('#map_detail').hide();}
$('#map_tabs li#map_'+map_type+' a').addClass("here");}}
function loadBMap(){if(get('bmap_iframe_loaded')===false){set('bmap_iframe_loaded',true);$('#bmap').append('&lt;iframe id="bmap_iframe" src="" scrolling="no" frameborder="0"&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;');$('iframe#bmap_iframe').attr('src','/static/bmap.htm');$('iframe#bmap_iframe').load(function(){loadBMapDetail();});}else{loadBMapDetail();}}
function loadBMapDetail(){document.getElementById('bmap_iframe').contentWindow.geo_lat=geo_lat;document.getElementById('bmap_iframe').contentWindow.geo_lon=geo_lon;var message=InfoWindowHtml(listing_id,-1,display_price,addr_line1,addr_line2,map_image,'/listing/from_listing_map',address_displayable,geo_precision,display_address,idx_logo,bedrooms,bathrooms,square_feet,mls_number,mls_board_id,images_count,reduced,recent,0,ga_extra_info,'');document.getElementById('bmap_iframe').contentWindow.info_html=message;document.getElementById('bmap_iframe').contentWindow.loadInnerBMap();}

function track_event(category,action,label,value){ga('send','event',category,action,label?String(label):undefined,value?parseInt(value):undefined);ga('domain.send','event',category,action,label?String(label):undefined,value?parseInt(value):undefined);TL.main.get('analytic_pings')[category+'.'+action+'.'+(label?String(label):'')]=1;$.cookie("analytic_pings",JSON.stringify(TL.main.get('analytic_pings')),{path:'/'});}
function custom_dimension(dimension,value){if((dimension+'.'+value)in TL.main.get('analytic_pings')){return;}
var options=new Object();options[dimension]=value;ga('send','pageview',options);ga('domain.send','pageview',options);TL.main.get('analytic_pings')[dimension+'.'+value]=1;$.cookie("analytic_pings",JSON.stringify(TL.main.get('analytic_pings')),{path:'/'});}
function handle_page_tracking(){if(location.pathname.indexOf('/search')&gt;=0&amp;&amp;get_query_string('landing')!=1&amp;&amp;get_query_string('favs')!=1&amp;&amp;!get_query_string('mls_listing_id')){track_page('/list_view');}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('/search')&gt;=0&amp;&amp;get_query_string('favs')==1){track_page('/favorites');}else if(location.pathname.indexOf('/saved_searches')&gt;=0){track_page('/saved_searches');}}
return{track_page:track_page,track_event:track_event,custom_dimension:custom_dimension,handle_page_tracking:handle_page_tracking,get:get,set:set};});TL.recent_dropdowns.init(function(get,set){function display_previously_viewed(listings_viewed_obj){for(listing_viewed in listings_viewed_obj){if(listings_viewed_obj[listing_viewed]){$('#previously_viewed_'+listing_viewed).show();}else{$('#previously_viewed_'+listing_viewed).hide();}}}
function toggle_recent_listings(){if($('#recent-listings-more').is(":visible")){hide_recent_listings();}else{hide_recent_searches();$('#recent-listings-more').show();}
return false;}
function hide_recent_listings(){$('#recent-listings-more').hide();return false;}
function toggle_recent_searches(){if($('#recent-searches-more').is(":visible")){hide_recent_searches();}else{hide_recent_listings();$('#recent-searches-more').show();}
return false;}
function hide_recent_searches(){$('#recent-searches-more').hide();return false;}
function populate_recent_listings(json_info){var recent_listings_str='';var saved_listings_str='';var listing_str='';var recent_listings_counter=0;var saved_listings_counter=0;var img_uri;if(json_info.recent_listings){for(recent_listing in json_info.recent_listings){var listing=json_info.recent_listings[recent_listing];if(listing===null||listing==-1){continue;}
var is_saved=0;if(json_info.saved_listings!==null&amp;&amp;json_info.saved_listings[listing.id]){is_saved=json_info.saved_listings[listing.id];}
img_uri=listing.image_uri?'http://resizer.tigerlead.com/_tls_resizer/?h=45&amp;q=90&amp;url='+listing.image_uri:'/static/images/no_photo.png';var search=TL.main.get('search_url')+'&amp;domain_id=9515&amp;mls_listing_id='+listing.id;listing_str='&lt;div class="listing-container"&gt;'+
'&lt;div class="recent-listing-image"&gt;'+
'&lt;a href="'+search+'"&gt;&lt;img src="'+img_uri+'" border="0" alt="" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;'+
'&lt;/div&gt;'+
'&lt;div class="recent-listing-info"&gt;'+
'&lt;div class="recent-listing-price"&gt;'+
'$'+commify(listing.price)+'&nbsp;'+
'&lt;/div&gt;'+
'&lt;div class="recent-listing-data"&gt;'+
'&lt;a href="'+search+'" class="address"&gt;'+listing.full_address+'&lt;/a&gt;'+
'&lt;/div&gt;';if(is_saved==0){listing_str+='&lt;div class="recent-listing-save"&gt;'+
'&lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" id="save_listing_'+listing.id+'" category="Menu" event="Save Listing" onclick="TL.main.update_listing_addr(\''+listing.address_number+' '+listing.address_street.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\');TL.main.update_listing_id(\''+listing.id+'\');TL.main.update_post_reg_action(\'save_listing\');return false;" class="save display_save_listing"&gt;Save Listing&lt;/a&gt;'+
'&lt;/div&gt;';}
listing_str+='&lt;/div&gt;'+'&lt;/div&gt;'+'&lt;div style="clear: both;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';if(is_saved==1){saved_listings_str+=listing_str;saved_listings_counter++;}else{recent_listings_str+=listing_str;recent_listings_counter++;}}}
if(TL.main.get('user_is_registered')){$('#saved-listings-container').show();if(saved_listings_counter&gt;0){$('#view_all_favs').show();}}else{$('#saved-listings-container').hide();}
$('#recent-listings-counter').html(recent_listings_counter);$('#saved-listings-counter').html(saved_listings_counter);$('#listings-container').html(recent_listings_str);$('#saved-listings-container').html(saved_listings_str);}
function populate_recent_searches(json_info){var recent_searches_str='';var saved_searches_str='';var search_str='';var recent_searches_counter=0;var saved_searches_counter=0;if(json_info.recent_searches){for(recent_search in json_info.recent_searches){search_str='&lt;div class="search-container"&gt;&lt;div class="recent-search-data"&gt;&lt;a href="'+TL.main.get('search_url')+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].query_str.replace(/"/g,'&quot;')+'&amp;ob='+encodeURIComponent(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].sort_type)+'"  class="s-link"&gt;';var recent_searches_criteria=new Array();var search_id=json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].search_id;var search_params=json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].search_params;if(search_id===null){continue;}
if(TL.main.get('current_search_id')===0){TL.main.set('current_search_id',search_id);}
if(search_params.s_query){if(search_params.s_query!=''){recent_searches_criteria.push("'"+search_params.s_query.substr(0,30)+(search_params.s_query.length&gt;30?"&hellip;'":"'"));}}
if(search_params['s_types[]']){var listing_s_types=search_params['s_types[]'];var listing_types_str='';for(i=0;i&lt;listing_s_types.length;i++){if(i&gt;0){listing_types_str+=", ";}
listing_types_str+=json_info['s_types[]'][listing_s_types[i]];}
if(listing_types_str!=''){recent_searches_criteria.push(listing_types_str.substr(0,30)+(listing_types_str.length&gt;30?'&hellip;':''));}}
if(search_params['s_areas[]']){var listing_s_areas=search_params['s_areas[]'];var listing_areas_str='';for(var i=0;i&lt;listing_s_areas.length;i++){var area_id=listing_s_areas[i];var area_name=json_info['s_areas[]'][area_id];if(area_name==undefined){continue;}
if(i&gt;0){listing_areas_str+=", ";}
listing_areas_str+=area_name;}
if(listing_areas_str!=''){recent_searches_criteria.push(listing_areas_str.substr(0,30)+(listing_areas_str.length&gt;30?'&hellip;':''));}}
if(search_params.s_price_min||search_params.s_price_max){recent_searches_criteria.push('Price: '+(search_params.s_price_min?'$'+commify(search_params.s_price_min)+' - ':'Any - ')+(search_params.s_price_max?'$'+commify(search_params.s_price_max):'Any'));}
if(search_params.s_br){recent_searches_criteria.push(search_params.s_br+'+ beds');}
if(search_params.s_baths){recent_searches_criteria.push(search_params.s_baths+'+ baths');}
if(search_params.s_sf){recent_searches_criteria.push(search_params.s_sf+'+ sqft');}
if(search_params.s_yb_min||search_params.s_yb_max){recent_searches_criteria.push('Year built: '+(search_params.s_yb_min?search_params.s_yb_min+' - ':'Any - ')+(search_params.s_yb_max?search_params.s_yb_max:'Any'));}
if(search_params.s_garage){recent_searches_criteria.push(search_params.s_garage+'+ garages');}
if(search_params.s_ca){var days_on_site_crit_txt;if(search_params.s_ca&gt;100){days_on_site_crit_txt='More than '+(search_params.s_ca/100)+' days on site';}else{days_on_site_crit_txt='Less than '+search_params.s_ca+' days on site';}
recent_searches_criteria.push(days_on_site_crit_txt);}
if(search_params.s_has_photos){recent_searches_criteria.push('Has Photos');}
if(search_params.s_has_vt){recent_searches_criteria.push('Has Virtual Tour');}
if(search_params.s_reduced){recent_searches_criteria.push('Price reduced');}
for(var key in search_params){if(key.match(/^s_field_\d+/)){var adv_id=key.replace(/\D/g,'');var adv_val=search_params[key];var adv_val_str='';if(typeof adv_val==='object'){var first=true;for(var v in adv_val){if(first){first=false;}
else{adv_val_str+=', ';}
adv_val_str+=json_info.advanced_config_lookup[adv_id].values[adv_val[v]];}}
else{adv_val_str+=json_info.advanced_config_lookup[adv_id].values[adv_val];}
var crit_full=json_info.advanced_config_lookup[adv_id].label+": "+adv_val_str;if(crit_full!=''){recent_searches_criteria.push(crit_full.substr(0,25)+(crit_full.length&gt;25?'&hellip;':''));}}}
if(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].name!==null){search_str+='&lt;div class="save_name"&gt;'+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].name+'&lt;/div&gt;';}
search_str+='&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;'+recent_searches_criteria.join('&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;')+'&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;';search_str+='&lt;/a&gt;&lt;div style="clear: both;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';if(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].is_saved==0){search_str+='&lt;a href="javascript:void(0)" id="save_search_'+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].search_id+'" category="Menu" event="Save Search" class="save display_save_search" onclick="TL.main.update_search_to_save(\''+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].search_id+'\');TL.main.update_post_reg_action(\'save_search\');"&gt;Save Search&lt;/a&gt;';}else{search_str+='&lt;a href="'+TL.main.get('search_url')+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].query_str.replace(/"/g,'&quot;')+'&amp;ob='+encodeURIComponent(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].sort_type)+"&amp;edit="+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].search_id+"&amp;search_name="+encodeURIComponent(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].name)+'&amp;e_n='+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].e_n+'&amp;e_p='+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].e_p+'&amp;e_s='+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].e_s+'&amp;e_f='+json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].e_f+'" category="Menu" event="Edit Search" class="edit-search"&gt;Edit Search&lt;/a&gt;';}
search_str+='&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="clear: both;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';if(json_info.recent_searches[recent_search].is_saved==1){saved_searches_str+=search_str;saved_searches_counter++;}else{recent_searches_str+=search_str;recent_searches_counter++;}}}
if(TL.main.get('user_is_registered')){$('#saved-searches-container').show();}else{$('#saved-searches-container').hide();}
$('#recent-searches-counter').html(recent_searches_counter);$('#saved-searches-counter').html(saved_searches_counter);$('#searches-container').html(recent_searches_str);$('#saved-searches-container').html(saved_searches_str);}
return{hide_recent_searches:hide_recent_searches,hide_recent_listings:hide_recent_listings,display_previously_viewed:display_previously_viewed,toggle_recent_listings:toggle_recent_listings,toggle_recent_searches:toggle_recent_searches,populate_recent_listings:populate_recent_listings,populate_recent_searches:populate_recent_searches};});$(document).ready(function(){TL.main.execute_document_onload();if($.urlParam("go")){if($('#tiger_regions_container').is(":visible")){TL.search_forms.toggleContainer('regions');}

if($('#tiger_additional_features_container').is(":visible")){TL.search_forms.toggleContainer('additional_features');}}
